	<meta name="description" content="Small finch. Sharply pointed bill is pink in summer, grayish-brown in winter. Small head, long wings, and short, notched tail. Adult males in spring and summer are bright yellow with black forehead and wings. Females are dull yellow below and olive above with two distinct wingbars. In winter, they are drab, buffy-brown. Active and acrobatic. Sometimes in large numbers at feeders or on ground below. Found in weedy fields, cultivated areas, roadsides, orchards, and backyards.">

	<!-- ---------------- Identification and audio ---------------- -->
	<section class="Page-section Page-section--loose" tabindex="0" aria-labelledby="identification-heading">
		<div class="GridFlex">
			<div class="GridFlex-cell u-md-size1of4 u-lg-size1of6 u-showForMedium">
				<h2 id="identification-heading" class="Heading Heading--h2">Identification</h2>
				<div class="u-text-2">POWERED BY <a href="http://merlin.allaboutbirds.org/">MERLIN</a></div>
			</div>
			<div class="GridFlex-cell u-md-size3of4 u-lg-size5of6">
				<!-- Audio playlist -->
				<div class="u-mlm u-mbm u-pullRight">
					<div class="Playlist-listen">
							<a href="#Modal-playlist" aria-controls="Modal-playlist" class="Button Button--pill Button--huge Button--highlight">
								<svg class="Icon Icon--audio" role="presentation">
									<use xlink:href="#Icon--audio"></use>
								</svg>
								Listen</a>
							<a href="#Modal-playlist" aria-controls="Modal-playlist" class="Playlist-listenMore"> +12 more audio recordings</a>
							</div>
					</div>
				<!-- ID text -->
				<p class="u-stack-sm">Small finch. Sharply pointed bill is pink in summer, grayish-brown in winter. Small head, long wings, and short, notched tail. Adult males in spring and summer are bright yellow with black forehead and wings. Females are dull yellow below and olive above with two distinct wingbars. In winter, they are drab, buffy-brown. Active and acrobatic. Sometimes in large numbers at feeders or on ground below. Found in weedy fields, cultivated areas, roadsides, orchards, and backyards.</p>
					<div class="u-text-2 u-hideForMedium">POWERED BY <a href="http://merlin.allaboutbirds.org/">MERLIN</a></div>
				</div>
		</div>
	</section>

<!-- Send custom events for clicks on Languages and Donate in header -->
<script>
	(function() {
		var sendCustomEventToGoogleAnalytics = function(category, action, label, value) {
			try {
				if (typeof ga === 'function') {
					if (typeof ga.getAll === 'function') {
						var tracker = ga.getAll()[0];
						if (tracker) {
							if (typeof value != 'undefined') {
								tracker.send('event', category, action, label, value);
							} else {
								tracker.send('event', category, action, label);
							}
						}
					}
				}
			} catch (error) {
			}
		}
		var headerLanguageLinks = document.querySelectorAll('[data-lang]');
		if (headerLanguageLinks) {
			Array.prototype.forEach.call(headerLanguageLinks, function(el) {
				el.addEventListener('click', function() {
					sendCustomEventToGoogleAnalytics(
						'header', // category
						'click', // action
						'language' // label
					);
				});
			});
		}
		var headerDonateLink = document.querySelector('[data-header-donate]');
		if (headerDonateLink) {
			headerDonateLink.addEventListener('click', function() {
				sendCustomEventToGoogleAnalytics(
					'donate', // category
					'click', // action
					'header-donate' // label
				);
			});
		}
		var footerDonateLink = document.querySelector('[data-footer-donate]');
		if (footerDonateLink) {
			footerDonateLink.addEventListener('click', function() {
				sendCustomEventToGoogleAnalytics(
					'donate', // category
					'click', // action
					'footer-donate' // label
				);
			});
		}
		var teaserDonateLink = document.querySelector('[data-teaser-donate]');
		if (teaserDonateLink) {
			teaserDonateLink.addEventListener('click', function() {
				sendCustomEventToGoogleAnalytics(
					'donate', // category
					'click', // action
					'species-teaser' // label
				);
			});
		}
		var privacyPolicyLink = document.querySelector('#privacy-policy-link');
		if (privacyPolicyLink) {
			privacyPolicyLink.addEventListener('click', function() {
				sendCustomEventToGoogleAnalytics(
					'prefs', // category
					'click', // action
					'privacy-policy' // label
				);
				// console.log("Privacy Policy event logged.");
			});
		}
		var termsOfServiceLink = document.querySelector('#terms-of-service-link');
		if (termsOfServiceLink) {
			termsOfServiceLink.addEventListener('click', function() {
				sendCustomEventToGoogleAnalytics(
					'prefs', // category
					'click', // action
					'terms-of-service' // label
				);
				// console.log("Terms of Service event logged.");
			});
		}
	})();

	if (audioAssetsJson.hasOwnProperty('galleryAssets')) {

		playlistData.galleryAssets[0].asset = {
			assetId: playlistData.galleryAssets[0].assetId,
			mlBaseDownloadUrl: 'https://cdn.download.ams.birds.cornell.edu/api/v1/asset/'

<script src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/lichen-dist.ornith.cornell.edu/1.7.32/explore/js/explore.ui.min.js" type="text/javascript"></script>

<script type="text/javascript">
$(function() {
	var ref = document.referrer;
	
	// is the user coming from another species page like this one?
	var isFromSpecies = (ref.indexOf('species') !== -1 );

	var speciesListPrev = document.querySelector('[data-specieslistprev]');
	var speciesListNext = document.querySelector('[data-specieslistnext]');

	function localStorageAvailable() {
		var test = 'test';
		try {
			localStorage.setItem(test, test);
			localStorage.removeItem(test);
			return true;
		} catch(e) {
			return false;
		}
	}
	
	/*
	 * The window.performance.navigation API may be deprecated, so we may need
	 * to reimplement this later.  I'm confident we can find a solution.  For
	 * now, I've verified that this works in Chrome, Firefox and Safari. 
	 */
	function isReload() {
		return window.performance
			&& window.performance.navigation
			&& window.performance.navigation.type
				=== window.performance.navigation.TYPE_RELOAD;
	}
	function isBackForward() {
		return window.performance
			&& window.performance.navigation
			&& window.performance.navigation.type
				=== window.performance.navigation.TYPE_BACK_FORWARD;
	}


	/*
	 * Get the list context for this page:
	 * - if no local storage, no list context
	 * - if the user has done a refresh, or we're coming from the species page,
	 *   the list context is in session storage
	 * - if a list context is in local storage, move it from local to session,
	 *   and then use it
	 * - otherwise, clear the session storage
	 */
	function getAndManageListContext() {
		var result = null;
		if (localStorageAvailable()) {
			var key = 'ebird_species_guide';
			if (isReload() || isBackForward() || isFromSpecies) {
				result = sessionStorage.getItem(key);
			} else {
				result = localStorage.getItem(key);
				if (result != null) {
					localStorage.removeItem(key);
					sessionStorage.setItem(key, result);
				} else {
					clearListContext();
				}
			}
		}
		return result;
	}
	
	/*
	 * These functions are called from the "Change species" popup.
	 */
	function clearListContext() {
		sessionStorage.removeItem('ebird_species_guide');
	}
	function setListContext(value) {
		sessionStorage.setItem('ebird_species_guide', JSON.stringify(value));
	}
	

	// replace the regionCode with new regionCode
	var setRegionPath = function(regionCode) {
		// always update region, regardless of list context
		updateToolbarWithRegion(regionCode);

		// remove possible trailing slash
		var paths = window.location.pathname.replace(/\/$/, "").split('/');
		if (pageHasRegion) {
			if (regionCode.length) {
				// swap region
				paths[paths.length - 1] = regionCode;
				pageHasRegion = true;
			} else {
				// world
				paths.splice(-1, 1);
				pageHasRegion = false;
			}
		} else {
			if (regionCode.length) {
				// add region
				paths.push(regionCode);
				pageHasRegion = true;
			}
		}
		window.history.replaceState({}, '', paths.join('/'));
	};

	// if user changes region, update prev/next if there is no list context
	var updateToolbarWithRegion = function(regionCode) {

		if (speciesListPrev.hasAttribute('href')) {
			var prevPaths = speciesListPrev.href.replace(/\/$/, "").split('/');
			if (pageHasRegion) {
				if (regionCode !== '') {
					prevPaths[prevPaths.length - 1] = regionCode;
				} else {
					// world
					prevPaths.pop();
				}
			} else {
				// come from world
				prevPaths.push(regionCode);
			}
			speciesListPrev.href = prevPaths.join('/');
		}

		if (speciesListNext.hasAttribute('href')) {
			var nextPaths = speciesListNext.href.replace(/\/$/, "").split('/');
			if (pageHasRegion) {
				if (regionCode !== '') {
					// has region, replace with new region
					nextPaths[nextPaths.length - 1] = regionCode;
				} else {
					// go to world
					nextPaths.pop();
				}
			} else {
				// come from world
				nextPaths.push(regionCode);
			}
			speciesListNext.href = nextPaths.join('/');
		}
	};

	// on region change
	document.addEventListener('lichen:changeRegion', function(e) {
		setRegionPath(e.detail.code);
		regionCode = e.detail.code;
		var frequencyGlobal = document.querySelector('[data-frequency-global]');
		if (frequencyGlobal) {
			if (e.detail.code === '') {
				frequencyGlobal.style.display = 'block';
			} else {
				frequencyGlobal.style.display = 'none';
			}
		}
		var regionalData = document.getElementById('regionalData');
		if (regionalData && !e.detail.doNotScroll) {
			regionalData.focus();
			regionalData.scrollIntoView(true, {behavior: 'smooth'});
		}
		// track change region event
		sendCustomEventToGoogleAnalytics(
			'species page', // category
			'changeRegion', // action
			'region changed' // label
		);
	});

	var triggerMapLoad = function() {
		var event = new CustomEvent('lichen:load-map-range');
		document.dispatchEvent(event);
	}

	var triggerTableLoad = function() {
		var event = new CustomEvent('lichen:load-table');
		document.dispatchEvent(event);
	}

	var triggerBarChartLoad = function() {
		var event = new CustomEvent('lichen:load-barchart');
		document.dispatchEvent(event);
	}

	// load stats, barchart, map when scrolled into view
	var observeIntersections = function() {
		var ebirdSpeciesIntersectionObserver = new IntersectionObserver(function(changes) {
			changes.map(function(change) {
				var el = change.target;
				// check the lazy attribute and if it's intersecting the viewport
				if (el.hasAttribute('data-ebirdspecies-lazy') && change.intersectionRatio > 0) {
					// wait for the browser to idle
					requestAnimationFrame(function() {
						// remove lazy attribute
						el.removeAttribute('data-ebirdspecies-lazy');
						// load table
						if (el.hasAttribute('data-table-async')) {
							triggerTableLoad();
						}
						// load barchart
						if (el.hasAttribute('data-barchart-async')) {
							triggerBarChartLoad();
						}
						// load map
						if (el.hasAttribute('data-mapobs')) {
							triggerMapLoad();
						}
					});
				}
			});
		});
		// observe all elements with attribute data-image-lazy
		Array.prototype.map.call(document.querySelectorAll('[data-ebirdspecies-lazy]'), function(el) {
			ebirdSpeciesIntersectionObserver.observe(el);
		});
	};

	var listContext = getAndManageListContext();
	if (listContext) {
		listContext = JSON.parse(listContext);

		// update species navigation
		var speciesListHref = document.querySelector('[data-specieslisthref]');
		var speciesListNames = document.querySelectorAll('[data-specieslistname]');
		var speciesListPrev = document.querySelector('[data-specieslistprev]');
		var speciesListNext = document.querySelector('[data-specieslistnext]');
		speciesListHref.href = listContext.url;
		// the list name is shown in more than one place
		Array.prototype.forEach.call(speciesListNames, function(speciesListName) {
			speciesListName.innerHTML = listContext.name;
		});
		var index = listContext.speciesList.indexOf(speciesCode);
		if (index !== -1) {
			var regionPath = '';
			if (pageHasRegion) {
				regionPath = '/' + regionCode;
			}
			if (index !== 0) {
				previousSpeciesCode = listContext.speciesList[index - 1];
				speciesListPrev.href = baseUrl + 'species/' + previousSpeciesCode + regionPath;
			} else {
				previousSpeciesCode = '';
				speciesListPrev.removeAttribute('href');
				speciesListPrev.style.opacity = 0.3;
			}
			if (index < (listContext.speciesList.length - 1)) {
				nextSpeciesCode = listContext.speciesList[index + 1];
				speciesListNext.href = baseUrl + 'species/' + nextSpeciesCode + regionPath;
			} else {
				nextSpeciesCode = '';
				speciesListNext.removeAttribute('href');
				speciesListNext.style.opacity = 0.3;
			}

			// update filter list for species search
			var event = new CustomEvent('lichen:suggest-filter', {detail: {name: 'species', list: listContext.speciesList}});
			document.dispatchEvent(event);

			// clear list on surprise-me
			var surpriseMe = document.querySelectorAll('[name=surprise-me]');
			Array.prototype.forEach.call(surpriseMe, function(link) {
				link.addEventListener('click', function() {
					clearListContext();
				});
			});

			// listen for change to filter list
			var speciesFilters = document.querySelectorAll('input[name=species_filter]');
			Array.prototype.forEach.call(speciesFilters, function(radio) {
				radio.addEventListener('change', function(e) {
					if (e.target.value === 'list') {
						setListContext(listContext);
						var detail = {name: 'species', list: listContext.speciesList};
					}
					if (e.target.value === 'all') {
						clearListContext();
						var detail = {name: 'species', list: false};
					}
					// update filter list for species search
					var event = new CustomEvent('lichen:suggest-filter', {detail: detail});
					document.dispatchEvent(event);
				});
			});

		} else {
			// bird not in list, need to drop list
			setRegionPath('');
			var event = new CustomEvent('lichen:changeRegion', {detail: {name: langMap['generic.World'], code: '', doNotScroll: true}});
			document.dispatchEvent(event);
			// set region name (in toolbar)
			var regionNames = document.querySelectorAll('[data-regionname]');
			Array.prototype.forEach.call(regionNames, function(el) {
				el.textContent = langMap['generic.World'];
			});
		}

		// ready to load components
		observeIntersections();

		// get common names for prev and next
		getPrevNextComNames();

	} else {

		// now that we know there is no region context, we can load components
		observeIntersections();

		// get common names for prev and next
		getPrevNextComNames();

	}

	if (!listContext) {
		// hide List UI (label and icon/link)
		var listElements = document.querySelectorAll('[data-specieslistui]');
		Array.prototype.forEach.call(listElements, function(el) {
			el.style.display = 'none';
		});
	}

	if (listContext) {
		sendCustomEventToGoogleAnalytics(
			'species page', // category
			'view', // action
			'has list context' // label
		);
	} else {
		sendCustomEventToGoogleAnalytics(
			'species page', // category
			'view', // action
			'no list context' // label
		);
	}
	
	if (pageHasRegion) {
		sendCustomEventToGoogleAnalytics(
			'species page', // category
			'view', // action
			'has region' // label
		);
	} else { // must be global
		sendCustomEventToGoogleAnalytics(
			'species page', // category
			'view', // action
			'global' // label
		);
	}

	if (userId) {
		sendCustomEventToGoogleAnalytics(
			'species page', // category
			'view', // action
			'signed in' // label
		);
	} else {
		sendCustomEventToGoogleAnalytics(
			'species page', // category
			'view', // action
			'not signed in' // label
		);
	}

	// count species views
	sendCustomEventToGoogleAnalytics(
		'species page', // category
		'view', // action
		comName + ' - ' + speciesCode // label
	);

	var frequencyGlobal = document.querySelector('[data-frequency-global]');
	if (pageHasRegion) {
		frequencyGlobal.style.display = 'none';
	}

	// on species change
	$(document).on('typeahead:selected', function(e, suggestion, data) {
		if (e.target.name === 'species') {
			window.location.href = '/' + ['species', suggestion.code, regionCode].join('/');
		}
	});

	// audio play events
	document.addEventListener('lichen:audio-play', function(e) { 
		var assetId = e.detail.assetId.toString();
		sendCustomEventToGoogleAnalytics('ML audio', 'play', assetId, e.detail.assetId);
	});

	function sendCustomEventToGoogleAnalytics(category, action, label, value) {
		try {
			if (typeof ga === 'function') {
				if (typeof ga.getAll === 'function') {
					var tracker = ga.getAll()[0];
					if (tracker) {
						if (typeof value != 'undefined') {
							//console.log('sending', category, action, label, value);
							tracker.send('event', category, action, label, value);
						} else {
							//console.log('sending', category, action, label);
							tracker.send('event', category, action, label);
						}
					}
				}
			}
		} catch (error) {
			//console.log('ga error', category, action, label, value, error);
		}
	}

	function getPrevNextComNames() {
		var url = 'https://api.ebird.org/v2/ref/taxonomy/ebird?fmt=json&locale=' + sppLocale + '&species=';
		var speciesCodeArray = [];
		if (previousSpeciesCode !== '') {
			speciesCodeArray.push(previousSpeciesCode);
		}
		if (nextSpeciesCode !== '') {
			speciesCodeArray.push(nextSpeciesCode);
		}
		url += speciesCodeArray.join(',');
		var prevText = speciesListPrev.querySelector('span');
		var nextText = speciesListNext.querySelector('span');

		$.ajax(url, {
			headers: {
				'X-eBirdApiToken': 'jfekjedvescr'
			}
		}).done(function(res) {
			res.forEach(function(sp) {
				if (sp.speciesCode === previousSpeciesCode) {
					prevText.innerHTML = sp.comName;
				}
				if (sp.speciesCode === nextSpeciesCode) {
					nextText.innerHTML = sp.comName;
				}
			});

		}).fail(function(err) {
			//console.log(err);
		});
	};

});
</script>

</body>
</html>
